***мышь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мышь</a> (3837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мꙑшь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">myšĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*myšь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*muh₂s</i>. The computing term is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic loan</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mouse</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мышь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">myšʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мы́ши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мы́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мыше́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mouse (animal)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полева́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мышь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">polevája <b>myšʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">field mouse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летучий.html>лету́чая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мышь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">letúčaja myšʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bat</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летучий.html>лету́чие</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мы́ши</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:использовать.html>испо́льзуют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ультразвук.html>ультразву́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> ориенти́рования <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> полёте.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Letúčije <b>mýši</b> ispólʹzujut ulʹtrazvúk dlja orijentírovanija v poljóte.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Bats use ultra-sound for flight navigation.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>mouse (computer pointing device)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:компьютерный.html>компью́терная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мышь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kompʹjútɛrnaja <b>myšʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">computer mouse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>Мышь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:множество.html>мно́жество</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кнопка.html>кно́пок</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:назначение.html>назначе́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Myšʹ</b> iméla mnóžestvo knópok, naznačénija kotóryx on ne ponimál.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The mouse had a lot of buttons whose purpose he didn't understand.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мышь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">myšʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-як</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rat poison</i>.

***мягкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a> (1154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мѧкъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mękŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mękъkъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*minˀkakas</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mn̥k-o-kó-s</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*menk-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mingle</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rusyn_language" class="extiw" title="w:Rusyn language">Rusyn</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="rue">мня́гкый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="rue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mnjáhkŷj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">мя́ккі</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjákki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">м'яки́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mʺjakýj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">mêhek</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjáxkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мя́гче</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мягча́йший</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наимягча́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>soft</li>
<li>fresh</li>
<li>gentle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po otnošéniju k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative, with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>mellow</li>
<li>mild</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> phonology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> soft, palatal, palatalized</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjáxkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjáxko</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-мя́гко" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мя́гче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>softly, mildly, gently
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjáxko</b> govorjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put it mildly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выражаться.html>выража́ясь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjáxko</b> vyražájasʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put it mildly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjáxkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***мягкость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мягкость.html>мя́гкость</a> (13695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjáxkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***мякоть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мякоть.html>мя́коть</a> (16397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мякоть.html>мя́коть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjákotʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мякоть.html>мя́коти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мякоть.html>мя́коти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мякоть.html>мя́котей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(soft) flesh (of meat); pulp (of fruits)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мякоть.html>мя́коть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́ба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjákotʹ</b> zúba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dental [tooth] pulp, pulpa splenica</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>мя́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>коть</b>

***мясной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясно́й</a> (6817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́со</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjáso</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjasnój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пирога.html>пиро́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjasnój</b> piróg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">meat pie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скот.html>скот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjasnój</b> skot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beef cattle</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjasnój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясно́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясны́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясной.html>мясны́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meat store, meat market</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ныть.html>но́й</a></b>

Зализняка — 1b | .
<a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>Кра́ткая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> муж. р. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>образова́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остальной.html>остальны́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>кра́тких</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рм</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднительный.html>затрудни́тельно</a>.

***мясо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́со</a> (1314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*męso</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mḗms</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">meso</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">maso</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">mięso</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">meso</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">mensa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́со</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjáso</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мяса́</a></i>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́с</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> flesh, pulp</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tissue, flesh</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (cannon) fodder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушечный.html>пу́шечное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мясо.html>мя́со</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">púšečnoje <b>mjáso</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cannon fodder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мясокомбинат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мясокомбинат.html>мясокомбинат</a> (21101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясокомбинат.html>мясокомбина́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjasokombinát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясокомбинат.html>мясокомбина́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясокомбинат.html>мясокомбина́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мясокомбинат.html>мясокомбина́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>meat processing plant; meat packing plant</li></ol>

<p><b>мя́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тый</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мя-</b>; суффикс: <b>-т</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
</p>

***мять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a> (15362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*męti</i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">мѧти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">męti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помять.html>помя́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">измя́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смять.html>смять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rumple, to crumple, to wrinkle, to fumble, to crease</li>
<li>to knead
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размять.html>размя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razmjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мяч.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> (4236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*męčь</i>, related to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mjáxkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">м'яч</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mʺjač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">míč</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">mȇč</i>.
</p>

***на.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> (5)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*na</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂neh₃</i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg/220px-Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg/330px-Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/16/Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg/440px-Alphi_On_A_Tree_-_panoramio.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="3000" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пень.html>пне́</a> (a dog on a stump)</div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_4">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">na</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> onto, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> stol</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>onto</b> the table</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вь</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:положить.html>положи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Postávʹ/Položí tarélku <b>na</b> stol.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Put the plate <b>onto</b> the table.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сел</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стул.html>стул</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja sel <b>na</b> stul.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've sat <b>on</b> a chair.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> что-то.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nastupíl <b>na</b> što-to.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped <b>on</b> something.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́ну</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nastupíl <b>na</b> mínu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped <b>on</b> a land mine.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случайно.html>случа́йно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>na</b> tebja slučájno nastupíl, izviní.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped on you accidently, sorry.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жвачка.html>жва́чку</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nastupíl <b>na</b> žváčku.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I stepped <b>in</b> gum.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>Твоё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:висеть.html>виси́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючке́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стене́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tvojó palʹtó visít <b>na</b> krjučké <b>na</b> stené.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Your coat is hung <b>on</b> the hook <b>on</b> the wall.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повесить.html>пове́сили</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убийство.html>уби́йство</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne xočú, štóby <b>na</b> menjá povésili ubíjstvo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't want the crime to be pinned <b>on</b> me.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">places, only certain nouns</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> nearby, by (in the sense of near). Interchangable with <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> (which requires genitive case).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реке́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:озеро.html>о́зере</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́ром</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рой</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́ром</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>рыб</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My živjóm <b>na</b> móre/reké/ózere, v kotórom/kotóroj/kotórom živjót mnógo ryb.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We live <b>by</b> a sea/river/lake in which many fish live.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to, toward
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> póčtu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to the post office</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>ухожу́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsjó, ja uxožu <b>na</b> rabotu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's it, I'm going <b>to</b> work now.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двинуться.html>дви́нулся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:север.html>се́вер</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:затем.html>зате́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обратно.html>обра́тно</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On dvínulsja <b>na</b> séver, zatém obrátno.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He moved north then back.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:германия.html>герма́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двинуться.html>дви́нется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A jésli Germánija dvínetsja <b>na nas</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What if Germany moves towards <b>us</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбо́ры</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U tebjá dve minúty <b>na</b> sbóry.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You have two minutes <b>to</b> pack [your belongings].</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:благотворительный.html>благотвори́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компания.html>компа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:направленный.html>напра́влена</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улучшение.html>улучше́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Náša blagotvorítelʹnaja kompánija naprávlena <b>na</b> ulučšénije míra.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Our charitable organization is aimed <b>to</b> improve the world.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set out for (in the sense "to start an activity with the intention of finishing it"), to go for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иди́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дракон.html>драко́на</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смочь.html>смо́жешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убить.html>уби́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>по́ка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сначала.html>снача́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> квест <a href = vnd.unilang:выполнить.html>вы́полнить</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne idí <b>na</b> étovo drakóna, ty jevó ne smóžešʹ ubítʹ póka, tebé nádo snačála tot kvest výpolnitʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't go <b>for</b> that dragon, you can't kill it for now, you need to complete that other quest first.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладно.html>ла́дно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> прокача́лся <a href = vnd.unilang:достаточно.html>доста́точно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойду́</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:босс.html>бо́сса</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu ládno, ja prokačálsja dostátočno, tak što (pojdú) <b>na</b> glávnovo bóssa sejčás ja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Okay, I've levelled up enough, and now I'm set out <b>for</b> the final boss.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эй.html>Эй</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союзник.html>сою́зник</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ej! Ne nádo <b>na</b> menjá! Ja že tvoj sojúznik.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Hey, don't attack me (don't go <b>after</b> me)! I'm your teammate.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">duration, value, purpose</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> što?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what for?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удача.html>уда́чу</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto tebé <b>na</b> udáču!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm giving you this <b>for</b> good luck!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">А-а, дак <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удача.html>уда́чу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A-a, dak éto tebé <b>na</b> udáču.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Oh, this is <b>for</b> your luck.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> 500 <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поставить.html>поста́вил</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подведи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>na</b> tebjá 500 rubléj postávil, ne podvedí menjá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've bet 500 roubles <b>on</b> you, don't let me down.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́йте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропитание.html>пропита́ние</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Podájte <b>na</b> propitánije!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Give us something (money, food, etc.) <b>to</b> eat!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́таешь</a>? <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> алексе́я?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> kovó rabótaješʹ? <b>Na</b> Alekséja?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Whom do you work <b>for</b>? For Alexey?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> about, for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объявить.html>объяви́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программа.html>програ́мму</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On obʺjavíl prográmmu <b>na</b> slédujuščij denʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He announced a program <b>for</b> the next day.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> +accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> over; by; divided by
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>Шесть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>де́лится</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Šestʹ délitsja <b>na</b> tri — eto dva.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Six divided <b>by</b> three is two.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>де́лится</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹ <b>na</b> dva ne délitsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">five is not divisible <b>by</b> two</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> in, for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> sevódnja vsjó!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's all <b>for</b> today!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> závtra tebe takóje zadánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Here is a task that's ought to be completed by tomorrow.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остаться.html>оста́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xóčešʹ ostátʹsja tut <b>na</b> sevódnja?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Would you like to stay here <b>for the rest of</b> the day (i.e. <b>till</b> tomorrow)?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>Придёшь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́лю</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pridjóšʹ na slédujuščuju nedelju?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Will you come for (whole of) the next week?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> in, for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>Придёшь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pridjóšʹ na slédujuščej nedele?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Will you come the next week?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> on, upon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> stolé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the table</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сижу́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стул.html>сту́ле</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sižú <b>na</b> stúle.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I sit <b>on</b> a chair.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́т</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:героиня.html>герои́не</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On (sidít) <b>na</b> geroíne.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is <b>on</b> heroin.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only with certain nouns</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> in, at
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> póčte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the post office</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́те</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́те</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Izviníte, on sejčás <b>na</b> rabóte.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Sorry, he is at work.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́де</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> zavóde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the factory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:балкон.html>балко́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>na</b> balkóne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the (inside) balcony (of a theater)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>стра́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>краю́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бездна.html>бе́здны</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Strána stoít <b>na</b> krajú bézdny.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The country is <b>at</b> the brink of an abbyss.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">'<i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><b> <a href = vnd.unilang:украина.html>украи́не</a></b></i><b> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"></i></b><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na<b> Ukraíne</b></i><b> ― <span class="e-translation"></span></b>in</i> Ukraine</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> using a means of transport to get somewhere (while <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> is just 'to be in something')
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бусе</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прыгать.html>пры́гаем</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My obýčno <b>na</b> avtóbuse, i vot tepérʹ opjátʹ <b>na</b> njóm; sidím v njóm, stoím, inogdá prýgajem.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We usually go <b>by</b> bus, and now we've got <b>on</b> it again; here we're sitting, standing, and sometimes jumping.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> runs/operates only because of someone/something; works on, runs on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a> полфи́рмы <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>вся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случиться.html>случи́тся</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da <b>na</b> njóm polfírmy stoít, a to i vsja, ne daj bog s nim što slučítsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Half of the company or even the whole company <b>operates solely thanks to</b> the work he does, god forbid something bad happens to him.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компания.html>компа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:строитель.html>строи́телях</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> — жа́дины — <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сидя́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кресло.html>кре́слах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>получа́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> бо́льше, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> трюдя́ги.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ix kompánija stoít <b>na</b> stroíteljax, a oní — žádiny — sidját na kréslax svoíx i pri étom polučájut v désjatʹ raz bólʹše, čem trjudjági.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Their company <b>lives only because they have </b> construction workers, nevertheless they—the greedy guys—just sit on their chair, and yet get ten times more money than the sloggers.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́тер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:электричество.html>электри́честве</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> ко́ка-ко́ле.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dánnyj kompʹjúter rabótajet ne na elektríčestve, a na kóka-kóle.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This computer runs not <b>on</b> electricity, but <b>on</b> cola.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> is assigned to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хня</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́т</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:однако.html>одна́ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хнею</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>поро́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заниматься.html>занима́ется</a> заме́сто <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хотя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>прошу́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> mne (stoít) kúxnja, a <b>na</b> nej (stoját) déti, odnáko i kúxneju oná poróju dáže zanimájetsja zamésto menjá, xotjá jejó tovó i ne prošú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I do the kitchen, while she raises children, yet sometimes she does my work without me asking her for.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дочь.html>дочь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чером</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вернуться.html>верну́сь</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Na</b> tebé dočʹ mojá, poká ja véčerom ne vernúsʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Look after my daughter until I come back in the evening.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> with, for</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism<span class="ib-comma">,</span> +prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> being dominated by a certain emotional state
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>вся́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвах</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказывать.html>расска́зывай</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случиться.html>случи́лось</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vsjá <b>na</b> nérvax, rasskázyvaj, štó u tebjá tam slučílosʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm so freaking <b>nervous</b>, tell me what happened to you.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вчерашний.html>вчера́шнего</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приставать.html>пристава́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On i tak <b>na</b> nérvax pósle včerášnevo, ne pristaváj k nemú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is already <b>on edge</b> after what happened yesterday, don't bug him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism<span class="ib-comma">,</span> +prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> accomplishing something while being dominated by a certain emotional state <b>and</b> primarily because of it
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неожиданно.html>неожи́данно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проиграть.html>проигра́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подряд.html>подря́д</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охватить.html>охвати́ла</a> дизмора́ль (<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́лась</a> дизмора́ль), <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проиграть.html>проигра́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́е</a> 8 <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neožídanno proigráv tri ráza podrjád, jevo oxvatila dizmorálʹ (u nevó pojavílasʹ dizmorálʹ), i <b>na nej</b> proigrál i vse drugíje 8 raz.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">After he had suddenly lost 3 times in a row, he got dismoral, and <b>while being affected by it</b> he lost all the remaining 8 times.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́лись</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достях</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дует</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> приоде́вшись, <a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошли́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:загс.html>Загс</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жениться.html>жени́ться</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pósle takój dólgoj razlúki, my ne uderžálisʹ, i <b>na rádostjax</b>, dáže kak slédujet ne priodévšisʹ, srázu že pošlí v ZAGS ženítʹsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">After such a long separation, <b>thanks to us being so happy</b> we couldn't hold it any longer and went straight to the marriage registrar's office in order to marry, without us even having dressed up appropriately.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сын</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ваш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:телевизор.html>телеви́зор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выкинуть.html>вы́кинул</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:специальный.html>специа́льно</a>… <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:эмоция.html>эмо́циях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:застать.html>заста́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> те́лик — <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвернуться.html>подверну́лось</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ponimájete li, syn moj vaš nóvyj televízor výkinul v oknó (iz okná) ne speciálʹno… prósto on byl <b>na</b> emócijax pósle tovó, kak zastál jejó, a télik — on prósto pérvoje, što jemú podvernúlosʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You see, my son threw your new TV set out of the window unintentionally… it's just that he <b>had such an outburst of emotions</b> after having caught her, that he had <b>had to do something</b>, and the first thing that crossed his mind was your new TV set.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">na</span>)

<ol><li>here! (said when giving someone something, i.e., "take it!")</li></ol>
